                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Air fried garlic French fries\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#airfriedgarlicfrenchfries #chips #friedgarlic #garlicpotatoes #airfryer #garlicfrenchfries #dry #garlicfies\n|hashtagrev=12032020\n|description=Delicious garlic flavoured chips; A few potatoes, a bulb of garlic and some olive oil\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=1st September 2021\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment =\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  40 minutes\n|PrepTime =  5 minutes\n|CookTime =  35 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 994\n|PortionCalories = 497\n|Image = [[Image:Air fried garlic French fries recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">So Simple, So Garlicky</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This could not be easier - garlic perfection!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n[[Garlic]] flavoured [[Chips|chips]]; lovely!  Saw this idea in a Gordon Ramsey Sunday Dinners TV program and as we always make our [[French fries]] in an [[Air Fryer|air fryer]], this was a no-brainer.\n\nA full bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] sliced in half is plenty - wrap the other half in [[Cling Film|cling film]] for the next time!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| Half a bulb of [[Garlic|garlic]] - sliced sideways to reveal all the [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| 4 medium sized [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Pinch of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Peel the [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| Cut them into [[French fries]] - we use a [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter]]\n| Rinse the [[Chips|chips]] well under running water\n| Leave them soaking in [[Salted|salted]] water until you are ready to cook them\n| [[Dry]] the [[Potato chips|potato chips]] in a [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] or a [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]]\n| Cook them at your [[Air Fryer|air fryer]]'s hottest temperature [200\u00b0 C / 220\u00b0] for 35 minutes or until golden.\n| Shake the [[Cloves|cloves]] out of the 'shell' of the [[Garlic|garlic]] bulb. Discard the shell and keep the golden [[Garlic cloves|garlic cloves]] to serve with the [[Chips|chips]] - Yum!\n}}\n\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries chips.jpg|Cooked to perfection - don't waste the lovely garlic cloves!\nImage:Air fried garlic French fries ready to cook.jpg|Ready to cook\nImage:Kuhn Rikon Salad Spinner.jpg|Use a salad spinner to dry the French fries\nImage:Potato chipper.jpg|This comes highly recommended - [[Sopito Stainless Steel Potato Cutter][\n</gallery>\n\n===Chef's notes===\nThis time of year, locally we are limited to [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]] but in season, Cara, [[Markies]], Agria, Mozart and Maris Piper make the best [[Chips|chips]]. &#127839;&#127839;&#127839;\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#airfriedgarlicfrenchfries #chips #friedgarlic #garlicpotatoes #airfryer #garlicfrenchfries #dry #garlicfies</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Apple Tart, French recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#appletart #butter #freerangeegg #tartring #apples #castersugar #lemonjuice #plainflour #miseenplace #doublecream #lemonzest \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A rich apple pie that can be made in just over an hour\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2746\n|PortionCalories = 457\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6 to 8\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Apple Tart recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Easy as...</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">... apple pie</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> - [[User:PSmith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nA rich apple pie that can be made in just over an hour.\n\n'''For the pastry:'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250g of [[plain flour]]\n| 125g of unsalted [[butter]]\n| pinch of [[salt]]\n| 1 [[free range egg]]\n| 1 tablespoon of cold water\n}}\n'''For the topping:'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 65g of [[caster sugar]]\n| 15g unsalted [[butter]]\n| 1/2 a tablespoon of [[lemon juice]] and half [[lemon zest]]\n| 3 or 4 [[apples]]\n| 100 ml of [[double cream]]\n| 1 [[free range egg]]\n| 5g [[icing sugar]] for dusting\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven and a baking tray to 220 \u00b0C\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix flour, butter and salt. Add the egg, water and mix again\n| Knead the dough for a few seconds, until smooth\n| Roll the dough to 2 mm thickness\n| Use a [[tart ring]] with a diameter of 20-22 cm to shape the dough, tucking it to the tart ring. Prick the bottom of the tart with a fork\n| Meanwhile, for the topping: heat the butter, lemon juice and zest with 15 g of sugar\n| Peel and cut the apples into segments and arrange them in circles\n| Brush the apples with the butter and lemon juice\n| Put the tart on the baking tray and bake for 10 minutes at 220 \u00b0C\n| Reduce the temperature to 220 \u00b0C and cook for another 20 minutes\n| While cooking, whisk the double cream, egg and the 50 g of caster sugar left. Sprinkle the tart with some sugar and pour the mixture on the tart.\n| Bake for further 10 minutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nLeave to cool for 1 hour, remove the tart ring and dust with icing sugar.\n==See also==\n* http://www.bbc.co.uk/food/recipes/appletartmamanblanc_93268\n* http://allrecipes.com/recipe/french-apple-tart-tarte-de-pommes-a-la-normande/\n* http://www.joyofbaking.com/AppleTart.html\n* http://www.epicurious.com/recipes/food/views/French-Apple-Tart-363307\n* http://www.telegraph.co.uk/foodanddrink/recipes/3315764/Kitchen-classics-apple-tart.html\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Apple Tart]]\n[[Category:Sweets_and_desserts]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#appletart #butter #freerangeegg #tartring #apples #castersugar #lemonjuice #plainflour #miseenplace #doublecream #lemonzest </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

try to find whole breasts, much easier for [[Stuffing|stuffing]]\n| 16 rashers of streaky [[Bacon|bacon]]\n| 5 [[Fat|fat]] [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]]\n| 1 very small white [[Onion|onion]], chopped very finely\n| 125g [[Camembert cheese|camembert cheese]] (half a 250g wheel) - I used Le Rustique [[Camembert]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| A splash of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] per [[Sous Vide|sous vide]] bag\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Bacon garlic, camembert, sous vide chicken saute butter.jpg|Saut\u00e9 in butter\nImage:Bacon garlic, camembert, sous vide chicken bath.jpg|Ready for the [[sous-vide bath]]\nImage:Bacon garlic, camembert, sous vide chicken rolled.jpg|Rolled up - they stay together really well after cooking in the bath\nImage:Bacon garlic, camembert, sous vide chicken bacon ready.jpg|Filled, ready for the bacon\nImage:Bacon garlic, camembert, sous vide chicken ingredients.jpg|The ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Peel and crush the [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| Finely chop the small white [[Onion|onion]]\n| Add to a small bowl with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and plenty of [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] and mix well\n| Cut a deep slice into the side of each breast to create a pocket\n| Use half of Le Rustique [[Camembert]] wheel, cutting it into eight pieces\n| Fill each [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] with equal amounts of the [[Garlic|garlic]] mixture and two pieces of [[Camembert cheese]]\n| I had a few spare [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]] so slices them and squeezed them in.\n| Lay four strips of streaky [[Bacon|bacon]] for each breast and carefully roll the breast up in the bacon.\n| Add a splash of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] (or [[Lime juice|lime juice]]) to each [[Sous Vide|sous vide]] bag.\n| Using a [[Fish slice|fish slice]] slide each [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] into the bag and seal - to save the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] being sucked out, press the seal only button the moment the [[Juice|juice]] starts to run up the bag.\n| Cook in a [[Sous vide bath|sous vide bath]] heated to 64\u00b0 C (147\u00b0 F) for 2 hours.\n| Remove from the bag, reserving any [[Juice|juice]] for making [[Gravy|gravy]].\n| Pan [[Fry|fry]] in [[Butter|butter]] for 3 or 4 minutes until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Air fried roast potatoes]], [[Steamed broccoli|steamed broccoli]] and a little [[Gravy|gravy]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n{{Template:Sous Vide, Smoking and Curing UK}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lemonjuice #camembertcheese #gravy #onion #baconwrappedgarliccamembertsousvidechicken #camembert #butter #chickenbreast #garlic #bacon #chickenbreasts </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Baguette",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baguette, French recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#baguette #fineyellowcornmeal #breadmaker #dough #bakingtray #eggwhites #bake #fats #sesameseeds #miseenplace #flour \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The baguette (French stick or French loaf) is a variety of French bread distinguishable by its much greater length than width, and noted for its very\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1319\n|PortionCalories = 87\n|DatePublished=8th March 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 15 - Makes 2 x 25cm (10\") baguettes\n |Difficulty = 1\n |ImageComment = Baguettes\n |TotalTime = 4 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours, 45 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour, 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Baguette recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">About the best I can make here</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not at all bad, but nothing like a baguette bought in a French bakery.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''The baguette''' ('''French stick''' or '''French loaf''') is a variety of French bread distinguishable by its much greater length than width, and noted for its very crispy crust. The standard girth size of a baguette is approx. 5 or 6 cm, but can be up to a meter in length.\n\nFrench food laws define bread as a product containing only the following four ingredients: water, [[flour]], [[yeast]], and [[common salt]]; the addition of any other ingredient to the basic recipe requires the baker to use a different name for the final product. As a result, the traditional baguette is made from a very lean [[dough]], made from a moderately soft flour. While a typical baguette is made with a direct addition of baker's yeast, it is not unusual for artisan-style loaves to be made with a poolish or other bread pre-ferment to increase flavour complexity, as well as the addition of [[whole wheat flour]] and other grains such as [[rye]]. French bread is required by law to avoid preservatives, and as a result baguettes quite frequently stale within a day of being baked.\n\nThis baguette recipe uses no [[Fats|fats]] or [[Oils|oils]], it has a delicious light airy texture and can be made in a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]].\n\nUse menu 21 ''French dough'' (3 hours 35 minutes) on [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried active yeast|dried active yeast]].\n| 250g (9 oz) [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]].\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| 1 tablespoon [[Milk powder|milk powder]].\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]].\n| 160 ml water.\n| 1 [[Egg white]] for glazing.\n| 15 g [[Sesame seeds]] or [[poppy seeds]] for sprinkling.\n| [[Fine yellow cornmeal]] for dusting.\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the ingredients to your [[Bread maker|bread maker]] on the [[French]] [[Dough|dough]] setting (or the longest dough setting available).  It's nearly 4 hours on our Panasonic SD 253.\n| Use menu 21 ''French dough'' (3 hours 35 minutes) on [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]]\n| Divide into 2 and roll into sticks.\n| Make 4 diagonal slashes in the top of the sticks.\n| Place on a [[baking tray]] that has been well dusted  , well spaced so they don't join together when [[Proving|proving]].\n| Leave of an hour or so in a [[warm place]] until doubled in size.\n| Brush with [[egg whites]] and sprinkle with the seeds of your choice.\n| [[Bake]] for 12 minutes or until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Remove and place on a rack to cool.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Fine yellow cornmeal]] is great for dusting the [[baking tray]] as it has a nice  look, taste and texture.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#baguette #fineyellowcornmeal #breadmaker #dough #bakingtray #eggwhites #bake #fats #sesameseeds #miseenplace #flour </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked Camembert a French cheese fondue recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheese #fondue #dip #vacherincheese #miseenplace #pickledredcabbage #bakedcamembert #gherkins #ciabattabread #pickledonions #newpotatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I discovered that we already had hint to the origin of this recipe on our Vacherin cheese page\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1078\n|PortionCalories = 269\n|DatePublished=1st November 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 1 hour\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:French cheese fondue recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nom, nom, nom!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You MUST try this - you will love me for it.  Hot melted Camembert - wowsers!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nI discovered that we already had hint to the origin of this recipe on our [[Vacherin cheese]] page.  However, a recent reading of [[The Extraordinary Cookbook]] finally brought it to my attention.\n\nI have substituted the marvellous [[Pi\u00e9 d'Angloys cheese]] for the [[Vacherin]] used in Stefan's recipe as it is available all year round and is as ridiculously cheap as it gorgeous.  If you want to try the original, [[Vacherin cheese]] is usually available from August and end of March. I believe it is available in the UK from Waitrose during this period. [[\u00c9poisses de Bourgogne]] is another excellent candidate for this recipe.\n\nYou could of course try this with more than one [[Cheese|cheese]], but that would be greedy, wouldn't it?\n\n'''the [[Fondue|fondue]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 box of [[Pi\u00e9 d'Angloys cheese]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n}}\n'''to [[Dip|dip]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 200 g Warm baby [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]]\n| 2 Sliced [[Ciabatta bread|ciabatta bread]] rolls\n| 150 g selection of thinly sliced cooked [[Meats|meats]]\n| 4 [[Pickled]] [[Gherkins|gherkins]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Pickled red cabbage]]\n| 2 [[Pickled onions]]\n| A selection of raw and [[Blanched|blanched]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Take the [[Cheese|cheese]] out of the box and line the box with a layer of good quality [[Tin foil|tin foil]] (some are better than others!)\n| Line the lid with tin-foil\n| Replace the [[Cheese|cheese]] in the box\n| Push the centre of the [[Cheese|cheese]] down to make a little 'well'\n| Use a fork to punch a few holes in the top of the [[Cheese|cheese]]\n| Pour the [[Sherry|sherry]] into the [[Cheese|cheese]]\n}}\n* Leave it for an hour or so if you have the time\n# Replace the lid and [[Bake|bake]] for 25 minutes\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Camembert fondue recipe.jpg|[[Camembert]] cooked\nImage:French cheese fondue sherry.jpg|The sherry soaking into the cheese\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nBreak the top of the hot cheese open, sit the [[Cheese|cheese]] in the middle of the table and surround it with your friends, lots of plates, napkins and things to [[Dip|dip]] into the cheese\n===Chef's note===\nI couldn't get [[Pi\u00e9 d'Angloys cheese]] the day I made this so I used what was available from a very limited selection of cheeses at our local supermarket.  This was so good - I would try it with any of your favourite cheeses!\n==See also==\n* Our selection of other [[Fondue|fondue recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheese #fondue #dip #vacherincheese #miseenplace #pickledredcabbage #bakedcamembert #gherkins #ciabattabread #pickledonions #newpotatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked whole Camembert with garlic, calvados and salami recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#garlic #calvados #salami #fondue #bake #bakedcamembertwithgarliccalvadosandsalami #dip #camembert #miseenplace #pickledredcabbage #newpotatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Whole camembert, packed with crushed garlic, calvados, covered with salami and baked in the oven. Dipping madness ensues!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2022\n|PortionCalories = 1011\n|DatePublished=14th February 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 1 hour 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Baked Camembert with garlic, calvados and salami.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Perfection!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Better than in a restaurant</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a meaty version of [[Baked Camembert]].  Just take a wheel of [[Camembert]] (or any similar [[French cheese]]), cut it in two, pack into two ovenproof dishes, fill with crushed or sliced [[garlic]], slosh on some [[Calvados]], cover with [[salami]] or similar and [[bake]] for 30 minutes.  Eat by dipping vegetables, breadsticks, anything really!\n\n'''the [[Fondue|fondue]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 box of [[Camembert]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Calvados]]\n| 4 cloves of [[garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 10 slices of thinly sliced [[salami]] or similar cold meat with a high fat content.\n}}\n'''to [[Dip|dip]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 100 g Warm baby [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]]\n| 2 Sliced [[Ciabatta bread|ciabatta bread]] rolls\n| 4 [[breadsticks]]\n| 2 [[Pickled]] [[Gherkins|gherkins]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Pickled red cabbage]]\n| 2 [[Pickled onions]]\n| 2 [[Spring onions]]\n| Sliced [[red peppers]]\n| Raw and [[Blanched|blanched]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]] - you get the idea...\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the cheese in half and place each half ovenproof bowls.  You could use one bowl. We wanted to customise our own!\n| Squash the cheese flat or cut a slash in it\n| Pack with crushed [[garlic]]\n| Pour over about 3 tablespoons of [[Calvados]]\n| Leave it to infuse for an hour or more\n| [[Bake|bake]] for 25 minutes\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Baked Camembert with garlic, calvados and salami added.jpg|Covered with [[salami]], ready for baking\nImage:Baked Camembert with garlic, calvados soaking and salami.jpg|2 different ways to infuse the cheese with [[calvados]] and [[garlic]]\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nBreak the top of the hot cheese open, sit the [[Cheese|cheese]] in the middle of the table and surround it with your friends, lots of plates, napkins and things to [[Dip|dip]] into the cheese\n==See also==\n* Our selection of other [[Fondue|fondue recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #calvados #salami #fondue #bake #bakedcamembertwithgarliccalvadosandsalami #dip #camembert #miseenplace #pickledredcabbage #newpotatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Baked squash filled with melted Camembert cheese",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baked squash filled with melted Camembert cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheese #squash #bakedsquashfilledwithmeltedcamembertcheese #bake #tacoshells #camembert #garlic #clovesofgarlic #tomatoes #baked #sherry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=We just love Camembert baked in the oven, dipping veggies or crisps into the melted cheese - mmm!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1443\n|PortionCalories = 721\n|DatePublished=1st November 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = My photography does not show how damned good this was!\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  1 hour\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Baked squash filled with melted camembert cheese recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Phwoarr!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The very idea!  Fabulous, though probably not very healthy if you took this regularly.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nWe just love [[Camembert]] [[Baked|baked]] in the [[Oven|oven]], dipping veggies or crisps into the melted [[Cheese|cheese]] - mmm!\n\nThis time I thought I would [[Bake|bake]] the [[Camembert]] inside the [[Squash|squash]], with plenty of [[Garlic|garlic]], obviously!\n\nI would normally suggest plain [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]] (''crisps'') to [[Dip|dip]] in the [[Cheese|cheese]], but every make I've tried recently is either ridiculously over-flavoured or just plain salty.  [[Taco shells]] have the same ingredients, but thankfully no added slat or flavours (yet!)\n\nI've pre-cooked the [[Squash|squash]] first as some [[Squashes|squashes]] take longer than others to soften and the dish would be pointless in a [[Rock|rock]] hard squash, over cooked squashes however, are fine.\n\nPre cooking the [[Squash|squash]] allows you to blot up any liquid released during cooking before you add the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n\nIf you know how long your [[Squash|squash]] will take to soften then you could [[Bake|bake]] it with the [[Cheese|cheese]] from the start.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 small [[Squash|squash]] ([[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] would be fine)\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, peelded and crushed or very thinly sliced - I used 3 [[Cloves|cloves]] to cook the [[Squash|squash]] and 3 to fill the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Salt]] & [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 whole [[Camembert cheese]] (I used a third of the wheel per person)\n| 2 tablespoons of [[shaved D\u017eiugas cheese]] (or [[Parmesan]])\n| 30ml of [[Sherry|sherry]]\n}}\n==== to serve====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 6 [[Taco shells]]\n| A few [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Baked squash filled with melted camembert cheese cheese loaded.jpg|The cheese loaded, ready for the last 15 minutes\nImage:Baked squash filled with melted camembert cheese part-baked squash.jpg|The squash, partially baked\nImage:Baked squash filled with melted camembert cheese ingredients.jpg|The basic ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Halve the [[Squash|squash]] top to tail (through the stem), [[Scoop|scoop]] out the [[Seeds|seeds]] and discard.\n| Crush a few [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]] with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]], mix with a few teaspoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and rub around the inside of the [[Squash|squash]].\n| [[Bake]] on an [[Oven tray|oven tray]] for 20 to 30 minutes or until it starts to soften.\n| Remove from the [[Oven|oven]] and use a [[Kitchen towel|kitchen towel]] to swab any excess liquid that may have formed during the cooking. \n| Cut the [[Camembert]] into thirds, and save the last third for another time. Crush another few [[Cloves of garlic|cloves of garlic]] and make a few random openings in the [[Cheese|cheese]] and  push the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] into the gaps.\n| Push the cheese into the squash, skin-side down.\n| Sprinkle with [[shavings of D\u017eiugas cheese]].\n| Pour a teaspoon of [[Sherry|sherry]] over each [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Bake|bake]] for a further 15 minutes\n| If serving with [[Baked|baked]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], drizzle each halve with [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]] and pop them into the [[Oven|oven]] with the [[Cheese|cheese]].\n| [[Microwave]] the [[Taco shells|taco shells]] for a few minutes to warm.\n| Serve!\n}}\n==See also==\n* [[Cheese fondue]] recipes\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:D\u017eiugas cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheese #squash #bakedsquashfilledwithmeltedcamembertcheese #bake #tacoshells #camembert #garlic #clovesofgarlic #tomatoes #baked #sherry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basic French loaf, French recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#breadmaker #basicfrenchloaf #panasonicsd253breadmaker #flour #strongbreadflour #breadrisingproblems #driedyeast #strongwhiteflour #butter #oliveoil #frenchbaguette \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is just a reminder to anyone with a breadmaker to try this recipe out\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1459\n|PortionCalories = 145\n|DatePublished=2nd January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 10 - Makes 1 loaf\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 6 hours\n|PrepTime = 4 hours, 30 minutes \n|CookTime = 1 hour, 30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Basic French loaf recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nThis is just a reminder to anyone with a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]] to try this recipe out.  Whilst it won't have the shape of a [[French baguette]], the flavour and texture is pretty close.\n\nWe have a [[Panasonic SD253 breadmaker]] and it is wonderful.  We have used it twice a week for the last year or so to make white or wholemeal loaves.  However, we have only recently tried some of the other recipes that came with the breadmaker.  Wow, they are really good.\n\nIf you have a Panasonic [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]], '''I urge you to try this recipe out!'''.  Also, if you wish to use genuine French bread [[flour]], it can be obtained from [[Wessexmill.co.uk|Wessex Flour Mill]] or one of their suppliers\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 teaspoon [[Dried yeast|dried yeast]]\n| 400 g (14 oz) Very [[Strong white flour|strong white flour]]\n| 15 g (1/2 oz) [[Butter|butter]] - don't be tempted to use [[olive oil]], it does not work as well for this recipe.\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 280 ml water - or by weight instead of volume, 280 g water\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Tip is all into the [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]]\n| For the [[Panasonic SD253 breadmaker]], Select '''French Bake''' program\n| For the [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]] use menu option 08, French bake\n| Wait 6 hours for closest you'll ever get to French [[Bread|bread]]\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nIf this loaf does not rise properly and you are using in-date [[yeast]] and [[strong bread flour]] and then it might be problem with your [[breadmaker]].  With our late [[Panasonic SD253 breadmaker]], this was the recipe that failed to rise, when all other recipes seemed to work.  Eventually this was cured by the replacement: [[Panasonic SD-ZB2502 automatic breadmaker]].\n\n* See also: [[Bread rising problems]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Breadmaking Perfection</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Since I added this recipe , seven years ago, we've probably used it three times a week since then.  The long rise time makes for a lovely light loaf, and as you don't have to do anything while it bakes, you may as well go for the longer bake to obtain the perfect loaf.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|French loaf]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|French loaf]]\n[[Category:Breadmaker recipes|French loaf]]\n[[Category:French recipes|French loaf]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#breadmaker #basicfrenchloaf #panasonicsd253breadmaker #flour #strongbreadflour #breadrisingproblems #driedyeast #strongwhiteflour #butter #oliveoil #frenchbaguette </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Basic fruit flan",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basic fruit flan recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#icingsugar #butter #dough #vanillaextract #cream #eggs #flour #clingfilm #basicfruitflan #berries #boil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A delicious fruit flan which is quite easy, but just be a little careful when making the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re. It is made using p\u00e2te sucr\u00e9e (with\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3927\n|PortionCalories = 654\n|DatePublished=7th June 2015\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  25 minutes\n|CookTime =  50 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Basic fruit flan recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Looks lovely Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A work of art that is beyond me!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA delicious [[Fruit|fruit]] flan which is quite easy, but just be a little careful when making the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re.  It is made using p\u00e2te sucr\u00e9e (with [[Ground almonds|ground almonds]]), but you can also make with p\u00e2te sabl\u00e9e (trickier) or p\u00e2te \u00e0 foncer (easier).\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====For the p\u00e2te sucr\u00e9e====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 190g [[Plain flour|plain flour]], sieved\n| 60g [[Ground almonds|ground almonds]]\n| 100g [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]], sieved\n| 100g [[Butter|butter]], cubed\n| 2 medium [[Eggs|eggs]] (room temperature)\n}}\n====For the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 medium [[Egg|egg]], plus 1 [[Yolk|yolk]] (room temperature)\n| 75g [[Caster Sugar|caster sugar]]\n| 45g [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 500ml [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]]\n}}\n====For the Chantilly cream====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 250g [[Double Cream|double cream]], chilled \n| 50g [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]] \n}}\n====To finish====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 600g fresh [[Berries|berries]], cut in half if using large [[Strawberries|strawberries]]\n| 10 g [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Grease (and line if necessary) a 23cm / 9 inch fluted flan tin or ring\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====For the p\u00e2te sucr\u00e9e====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[Flour|flour]], [[Almonds|almonds]] and [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]] in a bowl.\n| Rub in the [[Butter|butter]] until the mixture is like fine [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| Add the [[Eggs|eggs]] and mix gently to a smooth paste.\n| The [[Dough|dough]] will be sticky, but if too sticky, add a little more [[Flour|flour]]\n| Shape the [[Dough|dough]] into a [[Cow|cow]] pat, wrap in [[Cling Film|cling film]] and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 30 minutes.\n| Pre-heat the pven to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 170\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n| Roll out the [[Dough|dough]] into a rough circle and line the flan tin or ring.\n| Using a fork, prick the base.\n| [[Bake]] blind for 25 minutes, then bake for a further 15 minutes without the [[Baking beans|baking beans]] or until cooked.\n| Remove from the tin and leave to cool on a [[Cooling rack|cooling rack]].\n}}\n====For the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Whisk together the [[Eggs|eggs]] and 25g [[Sugar|sugar]] in a bowl\n| Whisk in the [[Flour|flour]]. \n| Heat the [[Milk|milk]] in a pan with the [[Rest|rest]] of the [[Sugar|sugar]] and as soon as it\n| comes to the [[Boil|boil]], pour into the [[Egg|egg]] mixture, stirring constantly. \n| Mix well, then pour the mixture back into the pan with the [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]]. \n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] over a medium heat, stirring continuously.\n| Allow to [[Bubble|bubble]] for 2 minutes, then pour into a bowl or jug.\n| Cover with [[Cling Film|cling film]] and leave to cool. \n}}\n====For the Chantilly cream====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Whisk all of the ingredients in a chilled bowl until it has thickened.\n| Do not over-whisk or you will end up with sweet [[Butter|butter]].\n| Cover the bowl and keep in the [[Fridge|fridge]] until needed.\n}}\n====To finish====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Gently fold the Chantilly [[Cream|cream]] into the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re, using a cold, metal spoon.\n| Tip into the cool [[Pastry|pastry]] case and smooth the mixture out.\n| Arrange the [[Berries|berries]] over the top of the [[Cream|cream]] mixture and sprinkle some sifted [[Icing Sugar|icing sugar]] over the top.\n| Keep [[Refrigerated|refrigerated]].\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Loosely based on recipes by the Roux brothers in '''The Roux Brothers on Patisserie (1986)'''\n===Chef's notes===\nEach component of the recipe can be made the day before, but ensure that the [[Pastry|pastry]] case is wrapped and that the cr\u00e8me p\u00e2tissi\u00e8re and Chantilly [[Cream|cream]] are covered in [[Cling Film|cling film]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:French recipes|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted|Fruit flan basic]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered|Fruit flan basic]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#icingsugar #butter #dough #vanillaextract #cream #eggs #flour #clingfilm #basicfruitflan #berries #boil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

title": "Basque-style Puy lentils",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "\n<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basque-style Puy lentils recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#oliveoil #onion #lentils #bouquetgarni #basquestylepuylentils #france #parsley #pancetta #butter #boil #duckfat \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=As a keen surfer, we spent 15 years holidaying around Vieux-Boucau-les-Bains, in the Basque region of France. My version of the famous lentil dish.\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1516\n|PortionCalories = 252\n|DatePublished=6th July 2016\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  25 minutes\n|CookTime =  1 hour\n|Image = [[Image:Basquestyle Puy lentils recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Worth hunting these down</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not always easy to find sensibly priced Puy lentils, but it's worth the hunt as they are so much nicer than normal orange lentils.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>}}\n[[Image:Basque-style Puy lentils pre boil.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready to simmer]]\nAs a keen surfer, we spent 15 years holidaying around Vieux-Boucau-les-Bains, in the Basque region of [[France]].\n\nThis is my attempt at replicating the [[Lentil|lentil]] dishes found in this lovely area of [[France]] (and [[Spain]]!)\n\nThis would be made with [[Duck fat|duck fat]] and served with [[Foie gras|foie gras]] or [[Roast|roast]] [[Duck|duck]].  Not having any of the aforementioned to [[Hand|hand]] I'm using [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Butter|butter]] and I shall serve it with half a [[Crispy aromatic duck|crispy aromatic duck]] from our local [[Chinese wholesaler]]. Not entirely [[French]] then, but still delicious and a great basis for recipe customisation.\n\nThis can be made ahead of time and reheated in a [[Conventional oven|conventional oven]] or [[Microwave|microwave]].\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g [8 oz] [[Puy lentils]]\n| 1 [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and slashed halfway through and studded with 2 [[Clove buds|clove buds]]\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], peeled and cut into small cubes\n| 160 g [5.5 oz] cubed [[Smoked|smoked]] [[Pancetta|pancetta]]\n| 6 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]]\n| Big handful of freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Splash of [[White wine|white wine]] or [[Sherry|sherry]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Rinse the [[Lentils|lentils]] in a [[Sieve|sieve]] under cold running water\n| Pop the [[Lentils|lentils]] in a large pan, well covered with cold water and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. Use filtered water if you are in a hard water area.\n| Immediately the water boils, remove from the heat and drain in a [[Colander|colander]], discarding the water.\n| Give the [[Saucepan|saucepan]] a wipe round add the [[Lentils|lentils]] and cover with 1 litre [1.24 [[Pints|pints]]] of cold water.\n| Sprinkle in 1 teaspoon of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and add the [[Clove|clove]] studded [[Onion|onion]], the [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]], half of the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] and the chopped [[Carrot|carrot]].\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] uncovered for 15 minutes, skimming any scum from the surface as required.  Check from time to time and top up with [[Boiling|boiling]] water if it's getting low.\n| Remove and drain, discarding the [[Clove|clove]]-studded [[Onion|onion]] and the [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]].\n| Heat a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or [[Wok|wok]] with a generous pinch of [[Black pepper|black pepper]], half of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] off half of the [[Pancetta|pancetta]] until it starts to [[Brown|brown]].\n| Add the chopped [[Onion|onion]] and cook gently for 10 minutes.\n| Add the remaining [[olive oil]] and the butter together with the remaining [[Bacon|bacon]] and cook slowly for another 5 minutes.\n| Add the chopped [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a few minutes.  Once it starts to take the slightest colour, stir in the [[Lentils|lentils]] and [[Carrots|carrots]].\n| Allow the [[Lentils|lentils]] to re-heat, stir in the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], season and serve.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nI've served this with half a [[Shredded|shredded]] [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Crispy duck|crispy duck]], which cooks from [[Frozen|frozen]] in about 40 minutes.  Delicious!\n===Variations===\nUse [[Duck fat|duck fat]] instead of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] if you can get it.\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #onion #lentils #bouquetgarni #basquestylepuylentils #france #parsley #pancetta #butter #boil #duckfat </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Bean and roasted red pepper flan an egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cream #bake #beanandroastedredpepperflan #egg #nutmeg #redpeppers #diced #greenbeans #pastry #peppers #roasted \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe has been adapted from one by Michel Roux in his book, Pastry\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3072\n|PortionCalories = 384\n|DatePublished=22nd January 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment =\n |Servings = 8 as a first course or 4 as part of a [[Main course|main course]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour, 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Bean and roasted red pepper flan.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fancy Pants!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A lot of work to make this, but definitely worth the effort!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe has been adapted from one by Michel Roux in his book '''[[Pastry]]''' (ISBN 1844006204).  Michel's recipe uses [[Asparagus|asparagus]] and sem-[[Confit|confit]] [[Red peppers|red peppers]], but as asparagus is out of season and I can't be bothered to semi-confit the [[Peppers|peppers]], I have just [[Roasted|roasted]] therm and substituted the asparagus with fine [[Green beans|green beans]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 340g p\u00e2te bris\u00e9e \n| 170g fine [[Green beans|green beans]], trimmed, [[Boiled|boiled]] and drained\n| Seasoning\n| 5 [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]], skins removed and [[Diced|diced]]\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n| 2 [[Egg yolks|egg yolks]], beaten\n| 200ml [[Double cream|double cream]]\n| Pinch of [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| [[Chives]] or [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped, to garnish\n\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Roll out the [[Pastry|pastry]] thinly and use it to line a loose bottomed 35 x 11 cm and 2.5 cm deep tranche tin.\n| Place in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for 20 minutes.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 190\u00b0 C (375\u00b0 F - gas 5) and [[Bake|bake]] the case blind for 20 minutes.\n| Remove the [[Baking beans|baking beans]] and paper, reduce the [[Oven|oven]] to 170\u00b0 C (325\u00b0 F - gas 3) and [[Bake|bake]] the case for a further 10 minutes.\n| Cover the bottom of the case with the [[Diced|diced]] [[Red peppers|red peppers]].\n| Whisk the [[Eggs|eggs]], [[Cream|cream]], seasoning and [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] and pour three-quarters of the mixture over the [[Peppers|peppers]].\n| Arrange the drained [[Beans|beans]] over the top and then pour over the remaining [[Egg|egg]] and [[Cream|cream]] mixture - you may find, as I did, that you have some mixture left over.\n| [[Bake]] for 30 minutes and let wait on a wire rack for 20 minutes before unmolding.\n| Garnish with the chopped [[Herbs|herbs]] and serve warm.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Salad|salad]] and [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]].\n===Chef's notes===\nI would recommend placing the tranche tin on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] before putting in the [[Oven|oven]].  This is because the [[Egg|egg]] and [[Cream|cream]] mixture is runny and may escape through the bottom of the tranche tin and make a mess of your oven.\n{{Quiche - See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pies tarts and flans]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cream #bake #beanandroastedredpepperflan #egg #nutmeg #redpeppers #diced #greenbeans #pastry #peppers #roasted </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Beef bourguignon (slow cooker recipe) \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#carrots #redwine #beef #onions #bouquetgarni #slowcooker #mashedpotatoes #boeufbourguignon #celery #unusualrecipes #blackpepper \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A slow-cooker version of this delicious and well-known French beef stew recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3135\n|PortionCalories = 522\n|DatePublished=2nd June 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 8 hours 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 8 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Beef borguignon (slow cooker recipe).jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely with noodles</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And well worth the wait!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Beef bourguignon in the slow cooker.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After 10 hours in the [[slow cooker]]]]\n[[Beef]] bourguignon is a well-known, traditional French beef stew recipe. It is essentially a stew prepared with beef [[Braised|braised]] in a full bodied [[Red wine|red wine]] and [[Beef stock|beef stock]], generally flavoured with [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Carrots|carrots]], and a [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]], and garnished with pearl [[Onions|onions]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]].\n\nThis version is especially for a slow cooker and can be prepared with no pre-cooking and will cook in 8 hours (or more) so can be left cooking all day, while you are out at work.\n\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g [[Stewing]] [[Steak|steak]], trimmed of excess [[Fat|fat]] and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 3 large [[Carrots|carrots]], sliced in half length-wise.\n| 1 bottle of robust [[Red wine|red wine]] such as Bulls blood.\n| 225 ml beef stock made with 1 [[oxo cube]]\n| [[Bouquet garni]] (I used a variation on version 4)\n| half a lime (unsqueezed)\n| 8 [[banana shallots]], peeled and cut in half\n| 150g of [[button mushrooms]], sliced\n| 3 [[carrots]], scrubbed and sliced\n| 2 sticks of [[celery]] cut into moons\n| 110 g (4 oz) [[home smoked bacon]] or good quality smoked [[bacon]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[plain flour]]\n| Pinch of salt\n| Good pinch of freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n| 6 small tomatoes cut in half\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Season the flour with [[salt]] and [[pepper]]\n| Roll the meat cubes in the flour to coat well - this will help to thicken the stew.\n| Add the remaining ingredients to the [[slow cooker]]\n| Stir well\n| Cook on low for 8 hours or more. As an experiment, I left the stew as photographed for 10 hours (on low).\n\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\n\nOften served with [[noodles]], was also good with [[squash mash]] and garden peas. Also good with [[mashed potatoes]].\n\n===Variations===\nIf you have time beforehand, you can [[brown]] the whole [[shallots]] and the cubes of [[beef]] in a separate pan, before slow cooking. It adds a little colour and some extra flavour.  However, when testing this recipe, everything was tipped into the slow cooker, no pre-frying and the results were perfectly acceptable.\n==See also==\n* [[Boeuf bourguignon]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe (PC)]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#carrots #redwine #beef #onions #bouquetgarni #slowcooker #mashedpotatoes #boeufbourguignon #celery #unusualrecipes #blackpepper </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Beef bourguignon a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#carrots #bouquetgarni #beefbourguignonrecipe #onions #garlic #redwine #wine #buttonmushrooms #marinate #oregano #celery \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Beef bourguignon is a well-known, traditional French beef stew recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2913\n|PortionCalories = 728\n|DatePublished=1st June 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 3\n|ImageComment = Beef borguignon with squash mash and garden peas\n|TotalTime = 15 hours 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 12 hours 20 minutes\n|CookTime = 3 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Beef borguignon recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fabulous meal..</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..shame about the plate!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Beef borguignon marinade.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Simmering the marinade]]\n[[Beef]] bourguignon is a well-known, traditional French beef stew recipe. It is essentially a stew prepared with beef [[Braised|braised]] in a full bodied [[Red wine|red wine]] and [[Beef stock|beef stock]], generally flavoured with [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Carrots|carrots]], and a [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]], and garnished with pearl [[Onions|onions]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]].\n\nThis is my interpretation of this wonderful dish.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil]]\n| 400 g [[Stewing]] [[Steak|steak]], trimmed of excess [[Fat|fat]] and cut into bite-sized cubes\n}}\n\n'''Marinade'''\n* 2 sticks of [[Celery|celery]], cut into large pieces (they will be discarded later)\n* 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and quartered (will be discarded later)\n* 2 large [[Carrots|carrots]], sliced in half length-wise (these will be discarded later)\n* 750 ml robust [[Red wine|red wine]] such as Bulls blood. \n\n''' [[Bouquet garni]]''' (I used a variation on version 4)\n* 2 [[Bay leaf|bay leaves]]\n* half a lime (unsqueezed)\n* 1 sprig of [[Oregano|oregano]]\n* 1 sprig of [[Parsley|parsley]]\n* 1 sprig of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n* 3 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, bruised\n* 1 strip of [[Lime|lime]] peel\n\n'''Cooking the meat'''\n* 8 [[shallots]] or baby [[onions]]\n* About 100g to 150g of [[button mushrooms]] - ''1 small packet''\n* 2 [[carrots]], scrubbed and sliced\n* 110 g (4 oz) [[home smoked bacon]] or good quality smoked [[bacon]]\n* 3 tablespoons of [[brandy]]\n* Pinch of salt\n* 2 tablespoons of flour\n\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat 1 tablespoon of olive oil in a large pan. Add the onion quarters. carrots, celery and fry until the onion is softened.\n| Add the bottle of [[wine]], [[bouquet garni]] and bring to the boil.  Reduce the heat and simmer for 15 minutes.\n| Remove from the heat, allow to cool completely.\n| Arrange the steak in a bowl and pour the wine together with the vegetables over the steak and store in a [[refrigerator]] overnight to [[marinate]].\n| The next day, preheat the oven to 140\u00b0 C (275\u00b0 F - gas 1) \n| Drain the wine and reserve, pick out the meat and reserve, discard the remaining items.\n| In a large [[Dutch oven]], heat the remaining 2 tablespoons of olive and fry the bacon and onions for 3 minutes, add the carrots and mushrooms and fry for a further 3 minutes.\n| Pour in a splash of brandy and deglaze the pan.\n| Stir in the flour.\n| Pour in the reserved wine, add the meat and mix well and bring to the boil.\n| Remove from the hob, cover, place in the oven and cook for 2 hours.\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\n\nOften served with [[noodles]], was also good with [[squash mash]] and garden peas. Also good with [[mashed potatoes]].\n\n==See also==\n* [[Beef bourguignon (slow cooker recipe)]]\n* [[Boeuf bourguignon]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe (PC)]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#carrots #bouquetgarni #beefbourguignonrecipe #onions #garlic #redwine #wine #buttonmushrooms #marinate #oregano #celery </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Beef bourguignon recipe (PC)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Beef bourguignon a beef pressure cooker recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#bouquetgarni #garlic #onions #redwine #carrots #eggnoodles #beefbourguignonrecipe #boeufbourguignon #blackpepper #cornflour #oxocube \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Beef bourguignon is a well-known, traditional French recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2207\n|PortionCalories = 551\n|DatePublished=28th July 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |ImageComment = Beef bourguignonne with [[egg noodles]]\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes plus any marinading time\n |CookTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Beef borguignon and noodles.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A good cheat</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Was as good as my slow cooker effort.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n[[Beef]] bourguignon is a well-known, traditional French recipe. It is essentially a stew prepared with beef [[Braised|braised]] in a full bodied [[Red wine|red wine]] and [[Beef stock|beef stock]], generally flavoured with [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Onions|onions]], [[Carrots|carrots]], and a [[Bouquet garni|bouquet garni]], and garnished with pearl [[Onions|onions]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]].\n\nA WMF Perfect Plus 6.5 litre [[pressure cooker]] has recently joined my stash of [[kitchen tools|kitchen toys]] and I've been experimenting with the best way to cook beef bourguignon in a pressure cooker.  I was after a fully-flavoured dish rather than a fast one; this was the result.\n\nIf you want the authentic, non-pressure cooker version, [[Beef bourguignon recipe|you can find it here]].\n\n'''the marinade'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 300 ml full bodied [[red wine]]\n}}\n\n'''[[Bouquet garni]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 [[Bay leaf|bay leaves]]\n| 1 huge stem of [[cutting celery]], 'flowers and all' - A stalk of [[celery]], ideally with leaves would be fine\n| 1 sprig of [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| 1 small sprig of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n}}\n'''the stew''' \n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil]]\n| 3 large [[banana shallots]], peeled and cut in half\n| 4 cloves of [[garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 2 [[Portobello mushrooms]], (large field mushrooms), roughly sliced\n| 2 [[carrots]], peeled and chopped\n| 250 g [[Stewing]] [[Steak|steak]], trimmed of excess [[Fat|fat]] and cut into bite-sized cubes\n| 10 [[cherry tomatoes]] - any type will do, they happened to be spare\n| 2 tablespoons of [[tomato puree]]\n| Half an [[oxo cube]], crumbled\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n}}\n'''to thicken'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 tablespoon of [[cornflour]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 240g of dried [[egg noodles]], cooked as directed on the packet\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If you have the time beforehand, add the meat, half bottle of red wine, the cubed steak and the [[bouquet garni]] (tied with [[kitchen string]]) to a [[Lock and Lock]]-style box, cover, shake and refrigerate for a few hours or more.\n| Heat 2 tablespoons of olive oil in a large pan or wok.  You can use the pressure cooker for this but I've found it sometimes stick during the cooking so do any 'beforehand' saut\u00e9ing in my trusty [[wok]]. \n| Add a good grind of [[black pepper]], the [[shallots]] and the [[garlic]] and gently [[saut\u00e9]] 5 minutes, stirring now and then\n| Add the mushrooms and carrots and fry for another 5 minutes.\n| Tip the onions, garlic, mushrooms and carrots into the pressure cooker.\n| Add the meat and red wine marinade, reserving the [[bouquet garni]].\n| Crumble half an [[oxo cube]] into the cooker together with the [[tomatoes]] and [[tomato puree]] and stir well.\n| Sit the [[bouquet garni]] in the perforated trivet and sit this atop of the stew.\n| Cover and bring the pressure cooker to [[:Category:Pressure_cooker_recipes#Internal_temperature_related_to_pressure|high pressure]]\n| Cook for 1 hour\n| [[De-pressurising a pressure cooker|De-pressurise naturally]], during this time boil the noodles as directed\n| If the stew needs thickening, mix to a paste; a tablespoon of [[cornflour]] and  a tablespoon of cold water, stir this into the stew and bring back to the boil, uncovered, and stir for a minute or so.\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\nServe the beef over the noodles, discarding the bouquet garni.\n==See also==\n* [[Boeuf bourguignon]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe (PC)]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pressure cooker recipes]]\n==See also==\n* [[Boeuf bourguignon]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon (slow cooker recipe)]]\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bouquetgarni #garlic #onions #redwine #carrots #eggnoodles #beefbourguignonrecipe #boeufbourguignon #blackpepper #cornflour #oxocube </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I've made this again and again.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is just a bit of fun, as far as I am aware, there is no such thing as a Biarritz [[Omelette|omelette]], though perhaps there should be?  It was inspired by [[Biarritz potatoes]] and uses similar regional ingredients.  Having said that, and being a regular visitor to the area, I would say that [[Duck|duck]] rather than [[Pork|pork]] would probably be the [[Meat|meat]] of choice for this area.  Anyway, it was a very nice omelette\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Olive oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]], [[Roasted|roasted]]\n| 200g Good quality cooked [[Ham|ham]] or [[Gammon|gammon]], chopped\n| 4 [[Fresh eggs|fresh eggs]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* [[Roast]] the [[Red pepper|red pepper]], de-[[Seed|seed]] and rub most of the skin off, leaving a little of the burn skin for flavour.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Chop the [[Roasted red pepper|roasted red pepper]] and [[Ham|ham]]\n| Beat the [[Eggs|eggs]] and add a pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| ''Make 1 [[Omelette|omelette]] per person''\n| Heat 1 tablespoon of oil in a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] over a medium heat\n| Add a grind of [[black pepper]]\n| Pour in the [[Egg|egg]] mix and swirl the pan to distribute evenly\n| Cook for a few minutes on one side only\n| Once the edges start to solidify, tip in the [[Ham|ham]] and [[Red peppers|red peppers]], the centre of the [[Omelette|omelette]] should still be a little runny, see the picture\n| Serve immediately by tipping it onto a warmed serving plate, folding it on top of itself\n| By the time it gets to the table the 'runny' part will be perfectly cooked.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Chips|chips]] and [[Beans|beans]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFollow the [[RSPCA Think Pig Checklist]] to make sure that your [[Pork|pork]] has come from pigs that have been reared to higher welfare standards.\n* title": "Biarritz potatoes",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Biarritz potatoes, French recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#potatoes #biarritzpotatoes #parsley #ham #butter #boil #redpepper #roastgarlic #salted #peppers #roastedsweetpeppers \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Straight from the Aquitaine, where I must have spent 15 summers, surfing and windsurfing. My fave recipe from this area\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1400\n|PortionCalories = 350\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Biarritz potatoes.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">It's all made up!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Necessity is the mother of invention; that's my excuse for inventing this dish.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Biarritz potatoes recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Surfing in Biarritz]]\nStraight from the Aquitaine, where I must have spent 15 summers, surfing and windsurfing.  A wonderful area of [[France]] that the British seem to ignore. Markets and fresh produce everywhere, a great place for a holiday, unless it rains.  This dish is regularly cooked in the camper van!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 900 g (2lb) floury [[Potatoes|potatoes]] such as Desiree, King Edward, Nadine, Saxon or Wilja.\n| 50 g (1 oz) [[Butter|butter]]\n| 90 ml (6 tablespoons) [[Milk|milk]] or [[Single cream|single cream]]\n| 50 g (2 oz) cooked [[Ham|ham]], finely chopped\n| 1 large [[Red pepper|red pepper]], deseeded and finely chopped, though a selection of colours tastes the same but looks nicer.\n| 15 ml (1 tablespoon) fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and cut into small chunks so they cook evenly\n| [[Boil]] the potatoes in lightly [[Salted|salted]] water for 20 minutes or until very soft.\n| Drain the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and return to a low heat for a minute or two to dry out a little.\n| [[Mash]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] or pass thorough a [[Ricer|ricer]], beat in the [[Butter|butter]], [[Milk|milk]] and seasoning, then fold in the [[Ham|ham]], [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\n[[Roast garlic|Roast some garlic]] and squeeze the pure\u00e9 into the potatoes as you mash them.\n\n[[Roasted sweet peppers|Roast the peppers]] before chopping them.\n\nAny leftovers shaped into small patties and fried in [[olive oil]] make a rather good [[accompaniment]].\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe immediately\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#potatoes #biarritzpotatoes #parsley #ham #butter #boil #redpepper #roastgarlic #salted #peppers #roastedsweetpeppers </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Boeuf bourguignon",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Boeuf bourguignon a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#marinade #beef #boeufbourguignon #pork #bellypork #flour #bacon #boil #onions #parsley #garlic \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I have never made this traditional stew from Burgundy before, despite it being a 1970s classic in the UK\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3182\n|PortionCalories = 1591\n|DatePublished=1st June 2013\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 day, 3 hours, 45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 day, 45 minutes\n|CookTime =  3 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Boeuf bourguignon recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love this!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A bowl of this in front of a open fire is absolute bliss.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nI have never made this traditional [[Stew|stew]] from Burgundy before, despite it being a 1970s classic in the UK.  Finally got around to it and my husband thought it was great!\n\n'''For the overnight [[Marinade|marinade]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450g [[Stewing|stewing]] [[Steak|steak]], cubed\n| 1-2 tablespoons [[Dried|dried]] mixed [[herbs]]\n| 250ml gutsy [[Red wine|red wine]] - perversely I used DO Valencia, a Spanish wine\n| 1 tablespoon [[Brandy|brandy]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Stew|stew]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Plain flour]], seasoned with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 200g [[Belly pork|belly pork]], skin removed and reserved, and [[Meat|meat]] cut into smallish pieces\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 120g [[Pickled|pickled]] silverskin [[Onions|onions]], well drained (you can use fresh, but not available where I live)\n| 1 bulb [[Garlic|garlic]], finely [[Diced|diced]]\n| 100g streaky [[Bacon|bacon]], [[Diced|diced]]\n| 100g small [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]], wiped and left whole\n| [[Flat leaved parsley]], coarsely chopped, to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients in a bowl and leave overnight in the [[Fridge|fridge]], covered.\n| Remove the [[Beef|beef]] and [[Marinade|marinade]] from the [[Fridge|fridge]] and allow to come to room temperature.\n| Drain off the [[Marinade|marinade]] into a separate bowl and reserve.\n| Dry the [[Meat|meat]] with kitchen paper and place in a further bowl.\n| Lightly dredge with the seasoned [[Flour|flour]] (a [[Flour|flour]] dredger would be useful for this) and toss the [[Beef|beef]] in the flour.\n| Cook the [[Belly pork|belly pork]] (minus the skin) in a non-stick [[Casserole|casserole]] or [[Deep frying|deep frying]] pan until it starts to produce its own [[Dripping|dripping]].\n| Remove the [[Pork|pork]] pieces and reserve.\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], bring to a high-ish heat and add the [[Beef|beef]].\n| When the [[Beef|beef]] has [[Browned|browned]] on all sides, remove and reserve with the [[Belly pork|belly pork]].\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Bacon|bacon]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and cook until they start to colour.\n| Add the reserved [[Marinade|marinade]], and [[Boil|boil]] until the smell of [[Alcohol|alcohol]] has disappeared.\n| Add the reserved [[Pork|pork]], [[Beef|beef]] and [[Pork|pork]] skin.\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], then [[Simmer|simmer]] on a low heat, covered, for 2-3 hours.\n| About 15-20 minutes before the end, remove the lid and cook on a higher heat until the [[Sauce|sauce]] has thickened.\n| Serve, garnished with the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nYou can serve with [[Mashed potatoes|mashed potatoes]] and [[Vegetables|vegetables]].  Alternatively, I served with [[Rice|rice]] cooked in [[Beef Stock|beef stock]], to which I then added [[Butter|butter]] and more chopped [[Parsley|parsley]].\n===Recipe source===\n* Inspired by a recipe from Elisabeth Luard in her book '''Classic French Cooking''' (ISBN 9781840727241)\n===Chef's notes===\nI used a titanium [[Wok|wok]] to cook this dish and it worked very well.\n==See also==\n* [[Beef bourguignon (slow cooker recipe)]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe]]\n* [[Beef bourguignon recipe (PC)]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#marinade #beef #boeufbourguignon #pork #bellypork #flour #bacon #boil #onions #parsley #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Boule loaf",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Boule loaf, French recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dough #bouleloaf #clingfilm #flour #fridge #semolina #roasting #bread #yeast #baking #steam \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is simply a ball-shaped loaf which is basically made with the same ingredients as Pan con semola de trigo duro\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 826\n|PortionCalories = 82\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 10 - Makes 1 loaf\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 days, 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 days 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Boule loaf recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n======Best recipe review======\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lots of work</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">..but well worth the effort!</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nThis is simply a ball-shaped loaf which is basically made with the same ingredients as [[Pan con s\u00e9mola de trigo duro]].  The method, however, is different as a delayed fermentation method is used and you need to start it a day or two in advance.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250g strong plain [[Bread|bread]] [[Flour|flour]] (I used '''[[Wessexmill.co.uk|Wessex Mill's]]''' [[French bread]] [[flour]])\n| 250g hard [[Durum wheat|durum wheat]] [[Flour|flour]] (for [[Pasta|pasta]])\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]] \n| 2 teaspoons easy-[[Bake|bake]] [[Yeast|yeast]]\n| 275ml cold water\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix all the ingredients together and [[Kneading bread|knead]] using your hands or a [[Mixer|mixer]] with a [[Dough|dough]] hook. \n| Place in a bowl and cover with lightly oiled [[Cling film|cling film]]. \n| Put the bowl in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for 12-48 hours, to allow the [[Dough|dough]] to rise slowly.\n| Remove from the [[Fridge|fridge]] a few hours before you want to use it.\n| When it has doubled in height from the original size, simply place the [[Dough|dough]] on a lightly floured surface, and work your way around the edge, tucking in each edge in turn into the middle. \n| Handle it gently and do not knock it back first.\n| Once you have a roughly circular shape, squeeze the gathered edges together to produce a taut surface around the rest of the boule. \n| Turn it over onto a piece of [[greaseproof paper]] so that the squeezed seam is on the bottom of the loaf. \n| Cover it with oiled [[Clingfilm|clingfilm]]/[[Plastic wrap|plastic wrap]], and leave to prove at warm room temperature until approximately doubled in height.\n| Preheat the [[Oven|oven]], with a with a [[Semolina|semolina]] dusted [[Baking|baking]] stone or sheet placed on a middle shelf and a deep [[Roasting|roasting]] tin on the oven floor, to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8). \n| Just before you put the loaf into the [[Oven|oven]], pour some [[Boiling|boiling]] water into the preheated [[Roasting|roasting]] tin to provide some [[Steam|steam]]. \n| Remove the [[clingfilm]] and slide the loaf using a [[Semolina|semolina]] dusted [[Bread|bread]] paddle onto the hot stone. \n| After 10 minutes, lower the heat to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)  and turn the loaf round so it bakes evenly. It should be done in around 25 - 30 minutes, but check it after 20. \n| If it sounds hollow when you knock the bottom of the loaf, it is ready.\n| Leave the loaf on a wire rack to cool completely.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nBecause this recipe uses a long [[Fermentation|fermentation]] process, it is not really suitable for [[Breadmakers|breadmakers]].  You can try it (for mixing and kneading), following your manufacturer's instructions regarding the order of adding the ingredients to the machine, but the end result will not be the same.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:French recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dough #bouleloaf #clingfilm #flour #fridge #semolina #roasting #bread #yeast #baking #steam </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
